  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_23d2d4f2-6d7f-4608-8a3c-33d85b65e63e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<div class='communityQuestionAndAnswer'>
<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/226570">يا جماعة انا هتجنن , إزاى (أ) مات وقع من فوق السطح وكان متجوز واحدة اسمها روؤي وبعدين نكتشف انه هو هو الى بيحب علا وعايش مش فاهم فين الربط
لو قولتولي (أ) ده شخصية مستقلة أما ب و ج د هم شخصية واحدة ماشي اصدق
لكن المصيبة انه بيقول ان الاربع شخصيات هم فى الحقيقة شخصية واحدة طب ازاى 
فين الربط بين أ و الشخصية الرئيسية ؟! هل انا ضايع منه حلقة تربط الاتنين ببعض ؟
?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_226570'><a id="like_count_community_question_226570" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/226570?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">5 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F20317106">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/39573415-ruqaiya-jilani"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_100x100-259587f1619f5253426a4fa6fb508831.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/39573415-ruqaiya-jilani">Ruqaiya Jilani</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">لأ انت فهمت كل حاجة غلط. د هو لما كان طفل, ب لما بئى مراهق. اما ج و هو شاب, اللي بعد متجوز علا بنتهم ماتت بعد كام يوم و الحب بتاعهم مات و اتطلقوا و كل<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">لأ انت فهمت كل حاجة غلط. د هو لما كان طفل, ب لما بئى مراهق. اما ج و هو شاب, اللي بعد متجوز علا بنتهم ماتت بعد كام يوم و الحب بتاعهم مات و اتطلقوا و كل واحد راح لحالوو و بعد كل الصدمات اللي عاشها , بقى الانسان الكئيب, أ ! و المحاضر اسامة قالهم انو أ مات بعد ما لقى السعادة الحقيقية عشان كل واحد يلحق نفسه و يرجع البيت يصالح مراته المزعلها و يخطب حبيبته اللي مكسوف يقللها و يلحقوا نفسهم بس أ متماتش ده كان اصلا قاعد في المحاضرة بتاعت اسامة و اسامة قلو سلملي على مراتك رؤى. كل ده اتشرح بالتفصيل في اخر الكتاب وللا انت كنت نايم وانت بتقرأ؟؟ لول <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3667148232695765531"><b>**10 amazing heart breaking original starts**</b><br/><br/>OH MY GOD! What was that?!! <br/>It was such an emotional roller-coaster!! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412910187ra/11440694.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't remember the last time i've finished a book this long in less than 6 hours!!<br/>It was like i've been transferred into a world that consumed every part of me...heart,soul and mind, it was just.. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413822319ra/11567635.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't want to give anything away of the story because it would be great if the reader just went in blind so i'll be vague as much as i could.<br/><br/>I didn't know what to expect when i started</span>
  <span id="freeText3667148232695765531" style="display:none"><b>**10 amazing heart breaking original starts**</b><br><br>OH MY GOD! What was that?!! <br>It was such an emotional roller-coaster!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412910187ra/11440694.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't remember the last time i've finished a book this long in less than 6 hours!!<br>It was like i've been transferred into a world that consumed every part of me...heart,soul and mind, it was just.. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413822319ra/11567635.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't want to give anything away of the story because it would be great if the reader just went in blind so i'll be vague as much as i could.<br><br>I didn't know what to expect when i started reading this book but from the first page and first line i felt like i've fallen under a spell....there was something invisible pulling me in.<br><br>I had a lot of mixed feelings and reactions varied with each part and character of the book..<br>Here's how it went,through out the first part of the book i felt a lump in my throat and something heavy on my chest....then i was filled with joy and felt love in the air and had a goofy grin on my face....at the end i felt all of the above, it was like crying and laughing,screaming and jumping all over the place all at the same time! <br>Even through the funny moments there was a deep melancholy hidden between the lines that made me want to cry!<br>There was something invisible that played on a deep subconscious level,something that touched my soul and played with my heart, something that made me feel every little detail, every word and action ....Made me feel everything he felt and understand and excused his actions,like i was there with him, in his head!<br><br>every word had a deep meaning, it really made a difference for me and touched me so deep..it gave me hope, made me think and open my eyes to things i didn't see clearly, made me appreciate everything i took for granted! <br>There are various situations and details that happen to all of us everyday and we just bypass it without giving it a second thought or look but this book makes you see everything from a whole new perspective and analyzes them with some deep psychological aspect that makes you truly think about things you didn't give much attention to....that's the main reason why this book got to me that much!<br><br><b>"You don't fall in love with a look,a smile or anything like that...true love is the one that life has been preparing you for since the moment you were born...with the good and bad, with the fucked up relationships and the unforgettable wounds.love truly starts when the heart finally asks: "Am i not going to eventually rest and find what i've been looking for all along?!"...love is a psychological preparation...that's why the beginning is the most important stage with all its mess and insecurities because that's the stage we can truly give in when a certain moment comes"</b><br><br>And that ENDING!!! It was one of the best endings i've ever read ......HOLY HELL! I never in a million years would've expected this ending...the author literally made my heart stop and then brought me back to life!!! He knocked the breath right out of my lunges and gave it back slowly without mercy!<br>It was like a big puzzle that was building up slowly and nicely without you realizing it through out the story and by the end..<b>**BOOM**</b>..every single piece fell in it's right place to creat one perfect master piece!<br><br>Everything about this book was perfect.....the story lines,the characters that developed perfectly,the settings,the amazing writing that no matter how i write about it i won't give it it's right!<br>God, it was like i've been in a trance...i just kept staring at the book after i've finished and didn't know what to do with myself or with the feelings dancing in my chest!! <br>No one can truly tell you about this story, it can't be told it's an experience you have to live through it to truly feel it!<br><br>All in all, It was a perfectly mind and soul touching story nd i LOVED every single part of it! I'm really so happy and grateful that i've read that book! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412348242ra/11362083.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I tried as much as i could to translate some quotes in my status updates and i hope it did this book any good.(i doubt it :D) <br>I wanted to convey and share with you even just a little bit of the amazing feelings this book incited in me.<br>And i wrote the review in English just for all of my friends that don't know Arabic! <br>It's really a sham such an amazing book isn't translated into other languages! <br>I hope they will consider doing that soon! <br><br>Finally, kudos to the brilliant author!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413822896ra/11567742.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll stop rambling now, Sorry guys for all this talking,This is probably the longest review i've ever written....! :D</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7514052124021564570">Perhaps I had felt a little disappointed at first with the lack of proper Arabic, I was hoping that a novel could help me with my Arabic. However, when I read into the second chapter I realized that the reader had to truly feel and live what the characters were going through, therefore, it was best to be written in the spoken, easily understood and heartfelt Egyptian Arabic. Personally, chapter 5 was the most interesting as it was very real. By the end of chapter 6, I could actually guess the en</span>
  <span id="freeText7514052124021564570" style="display:none">Perhaps I had felt a little disappointed at first with the lack of proper Arabic, I was hoping that a novel could help me with my Arabic. However, when I read into the second chapter I realized that the reader had to truly feel and live what the characters were going through, therefore, it was best to be written in the spoken, easily understood and heartfelt Egyptian Arabic. Personally, chapter 5 was the most interesting as it was very real. By the end of chapter 6, I could actually guess the end, I managed to connect the dots. Which killed the suspense quickly for me, however, it was unexpected. <br /><br />I loved how easy to read it was, how real and relatable it was and definitely how it provides insight and answers, directly and indirectly. And most importantly, the unexpected ending. <br /><br />- Also, I do not apologize for writing this review in English, this is still how I would find it easier to express myself. </span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('m5tZo5yc/9kIh0Yi6U8caCjxRvMWqZNgrL5ivNc1YLp84XosJXd0GkQHYWJFu9BoOrt0cnphaTiBPflTSFBLfA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('00OepJLQ7ZsXDKTO9iPedelfi6rKKuorA7R+KbKOSKg0Ob0rKztmWFuMg45a1xJ1+xW5K6biEHMuN+XGLetjbg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
